				<script type="text/javascript">
			$J( function() {
				BindAutoFlyoutEvents();

				var $Window = $J(window);
				var $Header = $J('#store_header');
				var $ResponsiveNavWindowShadeCtn = $J('#responsive_store_nav_ctn');
				var $ResponsiveNavOverlay = $J('#responsive_store_nav_overlay');
				var $ResponsiveNavOverlayCtn = $J('#responsive_store_nav_overlay_ctn');
				var $ResponsiveNavOverlayBottom = $J('#responsive_store_nav_overlay_bottom');
				var $HeaderWrapper;
				$Window.on('Responsive_SmallScreenModeToggled.StoreMenu', function() {
					var bUseSmallScreenMode = window.UseSmallScreenMode && window.UseSmallScreenMode();

											if ( !$HeaderWrapper )
							$HeaderWrapper = $Header.wrap( $J('<div/>', {'class': 'responsive_store_nav_ctn_spacer'} ) ).parent();

						if ( bUseSmallScreenMode )
							$ResponsiveNavWindowShadeCtn.append( $Header );
						else
							$HeaderWrapper.append( $Header );


						if ( bUseSmallScreenMode )
						{
							$Header.css( 'visibility', 'hidden' );
							$Header.show();

							var nStartingScrollPosition = $J('#store_header').height();
							if ( $Window.scrollTop() < nStartingScrollPosition )
								$Window.scrollTop( nStartingScrollPosition );

							$Header.css('visibility', 'visible');
						}
									} );
				
				window.setTimeout( function() { $J(window).trigger('Responsive_SmallScreenModeToggled.StoreMenu'); }, 0 );

										var g_rgUserPreferences = {
							excluded_tags : [],
							excluded_content_descriptors : [3,4]						};
						
													g_rgUserPreferences['use_store_query'] = 1;
						
						g_rgUserPreferences['use_search_spellcheck'] = 1;
						g_rgUserPreferences['search_creators_and_tags'] = 1;

						if( $J('#searchform').length > 0 )
						{
							// default search support where the web page includes the search edit control
							EnableSearchSuggestions( $J('#searchform')[0].elements['term'], '1_5_9_', 'SG', 1, 'schinese', g_rgUserPreferences, '20231154' );
						}
						else 
						{
							// search support for the mobile client.  the mobile client has a native search edit control but relies on the web content to perform the query and show results
													}
				
				// make genre categories expand/collapse on mobile
				$J(document).on( 'click', '.popup_genre_expand_header', function ( event ) {
					if ( !UseSmallScreenMode() )
						return;

					event.preventDefault();
					var $Element = $J(this);
					var $Target = $J('.popup_genre_expand_content[data-genre-group=' + $Element.data('genre-group') + ']' );
					if ( $Element.data('group-expanded') )
					{
						$Target.slideUp();
						$Element.data( 'group-expanded', false );
					}
					else
					{
						$Target.slideDown();
						$Element.data( 'group-expanded', true );
					}
				});
			} );
		</script>

												<img src="https://cdn.akamai.steamstatic.com/steam/apps/296070/ss_9e166f234403d3d60ab956f440aab420ec4fc1e7.116x65.jpg?t=1619166679">

												<img src="https://cdn.akamai.steamstatic.com/steam/apps/296070/ss_168011b3f8cf4b10d79f017c084776c92e91fc39.116x65.jpg?t=1619166679">
											</div>
																					<div data-panel="{&quot;focusable&quot;:true,&quot;clickOnActivate&quot;:true}" class="highlight_strip_item highlight_strip_screenshot" id="thumb_screenshot_ss_256b9a4b2ff3806b07178317659ed7924b9c00a3.jpg">
												<img src="https://cdn.akamai.steamstatic.com/steam/apps/296070/ss_256b9a4b2ff3806b07178317659ed7924b9c00a3.116x65.jpg?t=1619166679">

                                        <div class="slider" id="highlight_slider">
                                            <div class="slider_bg">
                                            </div>

                                            </div>

                                    <script type="text/javascript">
                                        $J( function() {
                                            var player = new HighlightPlayer( {
                                                elemPlayerArea: 'highlight_player_area',
                                                elemStrip: 'highlight_strip',
                                                elemStripScroll: 'highlight_strip_scroll',
                                                elemSlider: 'highlight_slider',
                                                rgScreenshotURLs: rgScreenshotURLs
                                            } );

                                            $J('#highlight_slider_right').click( function() {
                                                player.Transition( true );
                                            });
                                            $J('#highlight_slider_left').click( function() {
                                                player.TransitionBack( true );
                                            });

                                            
                                                // swipe gesture handling for the media carousel

                                                // TODO: We may want to move all of this to the player class so it has built in touch gesture support.
                                                // First testing here as part of new mobile ux.

                                                var k_nElementWidth = 120;
                                                var k_playerItemClassName = '.highlight_player_item';
                                                var g_nStripWidth = 1440;
                                                var g_nMediaItems = player.m_elemPlayerArea.find( '.highlight_player_item' ).length;
                                                var g_TouchEventStart = null;

                                                // Handle left/right swipe on the media playback by moving forward or backward when the swipe completes
                                                $J('#highlight_player_area').on("touchstart", function (event) {
                                                    g_TouchEventStart = event;
                                                });
                                                $J('#highlight_player_area').on("touchmove", function (event) {

                                                    if ( typeof g_TouchEventStart == undefined )
                                                        return;

                                                    var xdiff = Math.abs( g_TouchEventStart.originalEvent.changedTouches[0].screenX - event.originalEvent.changedTouches[0].screenX );
                                                    var ydiff = Math.abs( g_TouchEventStart.originalEvent.changedTouches[0].screenY - event.originalEvent.changedTouches[0].screenY );

                                                    // To reduce unintended page scroll during a horizontal swipe block the default handler when it looks like the user
                                                    // is in the process of performaing a horizontal scroll
                                                    if ( xdiff > ydiff && ( typeof event.cancelable !== 'boolean' || event.cancelable ) )
                                                        event.preventDefault();

                                                });
                                                $J('#highlight_player_area').on("touchend", function (eventEnd) {

                                                    if ( typeof g_TouchEventStart.originalEvent.changedTouches[0] == undefined ||
                                                        typeof eventEnd.originalEvent.changedTouches[0] == undefined )
                                                        return;

                                                    var xdiff = g_TouchEventStart.originalEvent.changedTouches[0].screenX - eventEnd.originalEvent.changedTouches[0].screenX;
                                                    var ydiff = g_TouchEventStart.originalEvent.changedTouches[0].screenY - eventEnd.originalEvent.changedTouches[0].screenY;

                                                    // clear out the touch start event
                                                    g_TouchEventStart = null;

                                                    // ignore the swipe if it was short and could've been intended as a tap, or the
                                                    // direction was more vertical than horizontal
                                                    if ( Math.abs( xdiff ) < 20 || Math.abs( ydiff ) > Math.abs( xdiff ) )
                                                        return;

                                                    // we're handling this event
                                                    if ( typeof event.cancelable !== 'boolean' || event.cancelable )
                                                        event.preventDefault();

                                                    // move forward or backward but don't wrap as that would be a jarring user experience
                                                    if ( xdiff > 0 )
                                                    {
                                                        var $NextItem = player.m_activeItem.next( k_playerItemClassName );
                                                        if ( $NextItem.length )
                                                            player.Transition( true );
                                                    }
                                                    else
                                                    {
                                                        var $NextItem = player.m_activeItem.prev( k_playerItemClassName );
                                                        if ( $NextItem.length )
                                                            player.TransitionBack( true );
                                                    }
                                                });

                                                // when the thumbnail strip is swiped move the strip at a granular level
                                                // so it feels active.  The active image does not update because when testing the code to
                                                // make it change the active element it seemed annoying
                                                var g_nSwipeStartingPosition = 0;
                                                var g_nMaxScroll = g_nMediaItems > 3 ? ( ( g_nMediaItems - 3 ) * k_nElementWidth ) : 0;

                                                $J('#highlight_strip_scroll').on("touchstart", function (event) {
                                                    g_TouchEventStart = event;
                                                    g_nSwipeStartingPosition = parseInt( player.m_elemStripScroll.css( 'left' ) );

                                                    player.StopCycle();
                                                });
                                                $J('#highlight_strip_scroll').on("touchmove", function (event) {

                                                    if ( typeof g_TouchEventStart == undefined )
                                                        return;

                                                    // To reduce unintended page scroll during a horizontal swipe block the default handler when it looks like the user
                                                    // is in the process of performaing a horizontal scroll
                                                    var xdiff = parseInt( event.originalEvent.changedTouches[0].screenX - g_TouchEventStart.originalEvent.changedTouches[0].screenX );
                                                    var ydiff = parseInt( event.originalEvent.changedTouches[0].screenY - g_TouchEventStart.originalEvent.changedTouches[0].screenY );
                                                    if ( Math.abs(ydiff) > Math.abs(xdiff) )
                                                        return;

                                                    // move the scroll strip without changing the selected item
                                                    var nNewScrollPosition = parseInt( g_nSwipeStartingPosition + xdiff );

                                                    // check that we don't scroll past the ends
                                                    if ( nNewScrollPosition > 0 )
                                                        nNewScrollPosition = 0;
                                                    else if ( nNewScrollPosition < (-1 * g_nMaxScroll) )
                                                        nNewScrollPosition = (-1 * g_nMaxScroll);

                                                    // set the new scroll position
                                                    player.m_elemStripScroll.css( 'left', nNewScrollPosition + 'px' );

                                                    // we're handling this event
                                                    if ( typeof event.cancelable !== 'boolean' || event.cancelable )
                                                        event.preventDefault();
                                                });
                                                $J('#highlight_strip_scroll').on("touchend", function (eventEnd) {
                                                    g_TouchEventStart = null;
                                                    g_nSwipeStartingPosition = 0;
                                                });

										
                                            if( window.location.hash )
                                            {
                                                var ssid = window.location.hash.substr(1);
                                                player.HighlightScreenshot(ssid);
                                            }
                                        } );
                                    </script>
                                                            </div>
                        					</div>
				</div>
				<div style="clear: both;"></div>
			</div>
			</div>

		function ShowAllLanguages( elLink )
		{
			if ( typeof GetUsabilityTracker !== 'undefined' )
				GetUsabilityTracker().AddEvent( 1002 );

			$J('table.game_language_options tr').show();
			$J( elLink ).hide();
			return false;
		}

					<div data-panel="{&quot;type&quot;:&quot;PanelGroup&quot;}" id="game_area_reviews" class="game_area_description">
						<h2>评测</h2>
						<p>“As visual, explorable art, it’s masterful. As a puzzle game, it’s rewarding and taxing.”<br><a href="http://www.rockpapershotgun.com/2014/08/11/mind-path-to-thalamus-review/" target="_blank" rel="">Rock Paper Shotgun</a><br><br>“Stunning, intelligent, fun, Mind is a game that deserves to be remembered for a long time to come.”<br>5/5 – <a href="https://steamcommunity.com/linkfilter/?url=http://www.telegraph.co.uk/technology/video-games/video-game-reviews/11035890/Mind-Path-to-Thalamus-review.html" target="_blank" rel=" noopener">The Telegraph</a><br><br>“This game is fantastic. It’s a legit puzzle game. It is beautiful. Go out and buy it”<br><a href="https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=UZzUOECDA4Y" target="_blank" rel="">Jesse Cox</a><br></p>
					</div>
				
									<div class="game_page_autocollapse_ctn"><div class="game_page_autocollapse" style="max-height: none;">
											</div><div class="game_page_autocollapse_fade"><div class="game_page_autocollapse_readmore">展开阅读</div></div></div>
									<div id="contentForThisGame_ctn">
					</div>
									<div class="game_page_autocollapse_ctn collapsed"><div data-panel="{&quot;type&quot;:&quot;PanelGroup&quot;}" id="aboutThisGame" class="game_page_autocollapse" style="max-height: 850px;">
						<div id="game_area_description" class="game_area_description">
							<h2>关于这款游戏</h2>
							<h2 class="bb_tag">Change the entire environment!</h2>Wrapped in a mind-bending tale, the gameplay of “MIND” focuses on<strong> changing the very weather in order to solve puzzles</strong>: the player will cycle between day and night, modify the levels of fog and rain and even travel in time between seasons, changing the environment to advance the gameplay-driven story —indeed, the mechanics are directly related to who the protagonist is, what has happened to him and everything he is doing: a man trapped in his own mind, he must use all the tools at his disposition to escape to reality. Accompanied by the snarky yet heartfelt narration of this comatose patient, the player will guide him through fantastical forests, dark caverns and deceptive worlds of water and ice that directly relate to his emotional state at each point in his journey.<h2 class="bb_tag">Enhanced Edition Features</h2><ul class="bb_ul"><li>Play the game in Virtual Reality for a full immersive experience. VR support only for motion controllers (HTC VIVE and Oculus Rift + Oculus Touch).<br></li><li>Powerfull new Unreal Engine 4 engine gaining even 70% more performance in almost every level. <br></li><li>Steam controller, keyboard, gamepad and VR controllers 100% supported and configurable.<br></li><li>4 secret levels, redesigned interactive ending, narration and also an alternative ending.<br></li><li>More than 40 different, creative puzzles seamlessly integrated into the environment.<br></li><li>6 ways to affect the environment in order to solve the puzzles.<br></li><li>More than 25 distinct landscapes into with which you will be able to interact.<br></li><li>Turn day to night, make it so everything is covered by a blinding fog, summon incredible storms, travel to the past and make use of even more as of yet unknown mechanics.<br></li><li>More than an hour of voice acting that, while integrated into the gameplay itself, will tell you a whole story that is not about saving the world but about living through the pain of a father broken by his mistakes.<br></li><li>Face down imposing enemies by using your creativity and everything you have learnt along the way.<br></li><li>22 achievements full of Easter eggs and references.<br></li><li>OST and Artbook included.</li></ul><h2 class="bb_tag">Who are we?</h2><br>Developed by Carlos Coronado  <a href="https://twitter.com/krateos29" target="_blank" rel="">Carlos Coronado</a>, <a href="https://twitter.com/PlayerDng" target="_blank" rel="">Dani Navarro</a> y  <a href="https://twitter.com/LukaNieto" target="_blank" rel="">Luka Nieto</a>. Aditional code by<a href="https://twitter.com/L4D15" target="_blank" rel=""> Jose Ladislao</a>. Voice by Greg Nugent.						</div>
					</div><div class="game_page_autocollapse_fade"><div class="game_page_autocollapse_readmore">展开阅读</div></div></div>
				
				
				
					<div class="game_page_autocollapse_ctn"><div class="game_page_autocollapse sys_req" style="max-height: none;">
		<h2>系统需求</h2>
					<div class="sysreq_tabs">
									<div class="sysreq_tab active" data-os="win">
						Windows					</div>
									<div class="sysreq_tab " data-os="mac">
						macOS					</div>
									<div class="sysreq_tab " data-os="linux">
						SteamOS + Linux					</div>
								<div style="clear: left;"></div>
			</div>
				<div class="sysreq_contents">
							<div class="game_area_sys_req sysreq_content active" data-os="win">
											<div class="game_area_sys_req_leftCol">
							<ul>
								<strong>最低配置:</strong><br><ul class="bb_ul"><li><strong>操作系统:</strong> Windows 7 (64 bits)<br></li><li><strong>处理器:</strong> Core 2 Duo E4300 1.8GHz<br></li><li><strong>内存:</strong> 2 GB RAM<br></li><li><strong>显卡:</strong> GeForce 7600 GS<br></li><li><strong>DirectX 版本:</strong> 10<br></li><li><strong>存储空间:</strong> 需要 2 GB 可用空间<br></li><li><strong>支持 VR:</strong> SteamVR</li></ul>							</ul>
						</div>

				<div class="content">
					<div class="bb_h1">How many times will I kill her?</div>How many times will I kill her?<br>梦醒在虚无里，混沌，黑暗，绵延至永恒<br>似乎有些光影的碎片？<br>我是真实的存在着的吗？光的触感为何如此飘渺？<br>飓风，我好像还记得这样一个词。<br>然而我是谁，我为什么会在这里，飓风又是什么<br>回忆仿佛卷进黑洞，正如我走进面前未知的迷雾。<br><br><br>How many times will I kill her?<br>好像听见水的声音，听见自己落在洞穴里发出的回声<br>索菲亚？那是谁？我认识吗？<br>心头掠过一丝恐惧，不禁大喊出来<br>相片在面前隐隐泛着微光，似乎有什么力量阻挡着我看清这世界<br>是夜幕吗？<br>然而脚步没有思考的企图，径直走进面前闪着幽光的大门。<br><br><br>How many times will I kill her?<br>我好像在寻找些什么，索菲亚？<br>索菲亚！那是我女儿啊！<br>视野猛然清晰，步出深穴，面前是绵亘的山川与清澈的河流<br>只是天空似乎仍然一片混沌？<br>我不知道下一个门会通向哪里，我只知道，那里一定有我和索菲亚的一切。<br>我们的过去，现在，和时间尽头的乐章。<br><br><br>How many times will I kill her?<br>似乎慢慢清醒过来，然而喜悦从未试图降临<br>因为是我，是我没有保护好索菲亚！是我杀了她！<br>我绝望地奔跑在荒野上，躲避着身后百倍高的巨人<br>但是真的就没有救赎了吗？<br>一次也好<br><br><br>How many times will I kill her?<br>医院。<br>哦这一定是一切开始的地方，我和我的索菲亚。<br>茫然寻找着，一瞬仿佛游离在天堂，一瞬又跌回现实<br>死神？这是对我自己的试练，要救回索菲亚，一定要先杀死自己。<br>这是一场绝不能输的战役。<br><br><br>How many times will I kill her?<br>然而一切归于平静过后<br>又如何呢？<br>我似乎看见了自己和索菲亚在一起<br>我看见了<br>我看见了<br>看见了<br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><b>===============哇你居然看到这里了？===============</b><br>大半夜突然发神经乱七八糟地写了一些字，没有回去改韵脚和用法，随便写写而已<br>——其实只是不想好好写评测<br><br><b>以下正文</b><br>这是一款很出色的第一人称解谜游戏，新颖的剧情思路和精妙的风景非常吸引人，简单总结一下<br><br>优点：<br>+ 瑰丽的画面，对得起虚幻引擎，不像一些奇怪的游戏<br>+ 出色的音效，男主声音也很好听（x<br>+ 超现实的风格，新颖的理念<br><br>缺点：<br>- 谜题提示太少，部分地图非常难以找到需要的过关元素，导致解谜部分看起来很难，很多时候要猜很久才知道要干啥<br>- 这一点已经够了，因为这个中途弃坑两次，那个西班牙语的视频指南在我翻墙看了一次过后就没了，噫<br><br>评分：<br><ul class="bb_ul"><li>画面 10/10 绚丽的画面<br></li><li>音效 8/10 能够很好烘托环境的音乐和音效<br></li><li>操作 7/10 无可厚非<br></li><li>游戏性 7/10 有趣的解谜，但地图太大，提示太少，难度偏高，运气成分不少<br></li><li>剧情 7/10 其实并没有剧情，超现实题材也并不少见<br></li><li>重玩性 5/10 真的，好累，一点都不像再重玩一遍，不要管成就了<br><br></li><li><b>整体 7.3/10 出色的超现实解谜游戏</b></li></ul><br>===============15.9.16更新线===============<br>9.0小时！全成就！疯啦！<br>亲测忍者成就可以死一次√<br>其他你们自己去找指南，西语哦<br><br>以上					<div class="gradient"></div>
				</div>

													<div class="responsive_review_leftcol_ctn" id="ReviewContentsummary23882839_leftcol_ctn"></div>
				
				<div class="postedDate">
					发布于：2016 年 6 月 28 日																					<div class="responsive_purchase_source">
															Steam 直接购买													</div>
									</div>

								
				<div class="content">
					作为一个解谜游戏爱好者，冲着解谜和画面玩了这款游戏。然而画面并没有想象中的美，但看看风景也还行。<br><br>重点的解谜部分不太喜欢，感觉需要的不是智商，而是视力和方向感。<br>在玩《Portal》、《The Talos Principle》时，你会惊呼：“啊，我知道怎么过关了！”<br>而在这个游戏里，你会说：“啊，原来这里有条路！”或者：“原来通关需要的东西在那里！”<br><br>还有一个问题是每个小关的场景设计得很大很开阔，很适合看风景，但主角的移动速度实在感人，很多时间都耗费在无意义的跑路上，特别是跑了一大段路还没找到路或者通关所需要的东西时，有一种大喊一声辣鸡游戏直接退游戏的冲动。<br><br>					<div class="gradient"></div>
				</div>

				<div class="postedDate">

				<div class="content">
					这个游戏才叫真的“意识流”……<br>首先画面没的说，氛围惊人！我不得不承认这个游戏更具有梦境般的效果。<br>虽然看起来仿佛是梦境画面配上心理独白，但是实际上这个游戏确实是一个游戏，谜题是存在的，并且解法也非常新颖，很多地方真的是要动一动脑筋。<br>而且，解谜是没什么明显的提示的，都是需要细心观察和大胆尝试，实际玩一下就会觉得非常有趣。<br>再次感叹一下，效果真的是惊人，环境营造得让你如同置身于一个奇妙空间，个人认为这游戏已经接近艺术品的范畴了。<br><br>严重推荐！					<div class="gradient"></div>
				</div>

													<div class="responsive_review_leftcol_ctn" id="ReviewContentsummary13829258_leftcol_ctn"></div>
				
				<div class="postedDate">
					发布于：2015 年 1 月 4 日																					<div class="responsive_purchase_source">
															Steam 序列号													</div>
									</div>

								
				<div class="content">
					视丘之径，这周慈善包的游戏，网上的完整攻略挺难找的，反正我没找到<br><br><br>题材是进入精神病人的内心，完成他从扭曲到清晰的心路历程，没有恐怖的部分，只有你挠破头脑去想方法的地方<br><br><br>玩这个游戏千万不要否认你眼睛看到的东西，因为那必定是你解题的关键<br><br><br>可以看到画面非常用心非常唯美，同时玩的时候请不要抱怨你的风扇转动声<br><br><br>光影很吊<br><br><br>纹理很吊<br><br><br>洞穴里的水滴声非常真实<br><br><br>背景更是唯美的一比<br><br><br>但是回到前言……我们作为一个正常人进入一个精神病人的内心去完成他自我救赎的过程……<br><br><br>这意味着我们要以精神病人的思维来思考这个游戏（认真），不管你是不是，反正我玩了这游戏也快跟精神病人差不多了<br><br><br>祝各位早日通关，GG<br><br><br>抱着拍摄风景的想法下载游戏的我得到了很大的满足感，但是我的大脑CPU已经烧掉了，GG					<div class="gradient"></div>
				</div>

								<a href="https://steamcommunity.com/id/Mendou/recommended/296070/" class="vote_header tooltip" data-tooltip-text="阅读完整评测">
					<div class="thumb">

										<img class="review_source tooltip" data-tooltip-text="产品是通过 Steam 序列号激活的" src="https://store.akamai.steamstatic.com/public/shared/images/userreviews/icon_review_key.png">
					
					<div class="title ellipsis">推荐</div>
										<div class="hours ellipsis">
						总时数 10.4 小时											</div>
									</a>
				
				
													<div class="responsive_review_leftcol_ctn" id="ReviewContentsummary19514052_leftcol_ctn"></div>
				
				<div class="postedDate">
					发布于：2015 年 12 月 6 日																					<div class="responsive_purchase_source">
															Steam 序列号													</div>
									</div>

								
				<div class="content">
					说实话，我对这游戏并没有什么特别的感觉，只是觉得某些场景美，很美，仅此而已。至于剧情，抱歉，因为加强版中文字幕自带斩首断尾特质，我根本没看懂。。。<br><br>作为一款解谜游戏，它的很多设计应该都算挺巧妙的，但是巧妙并不等于优秀，全程除了一幅偶尔出现的会指路的画完全没有任何提示，每次遇到新的机关总是需要花上好长时间才能理解（也有可能无法理解直接在某地卡死弃坑），虽然无地图无提示的设定会增强游戏代入感，但是因此而来的游戏难度提高则很容易使玩家厌烦，不过增强版增加了选关功能，某种程度上算是补足了这一缺点，不过强迫症嘛，你们懂的。这游戏虽然整体流程不长，但是完全不看攻略的话还是需要花上一段时间（虽然我觉得凭我的智商不看攻略完全可能在中途卡到弃坑）。<br><br>作为一款步行模拟游戏，这款游戏相当出色。漂亮的户外风景设计、偶尔出现的轻松的BGM，就算没有VR设备，也能感觉到旅途的美妙和惊喜，有闲心的话没事进去到处逛逛看看风景也是极好的，至于纯脑力解谜什么的，这是硬核玩家干的事。<br><br>至于游戏优化方面，这个，虽然普通版直升加强版很良心，虽然加强版刚出前几天不停更新很良心，虽然加强版自带中文很良心，但是目前依然存在很多系统BUG，不影响游戏内体验就是了。<br><br>总而言之，如果你希望看看风景，体验一段绝美的旅途，那么这款游戏是极好的选择（记住一定要看攻略一定要看攻略一定要看攻略），如果你并没有到处逛逛的闲心和耐心，那么这游戏并不适合你，毕竟风景美的游戏不只有这一款，而这款游戏除了风景美以外基本一无是处（这个奔着解谜来的你们开心就好）。					<div class="gradient"></div>
				</div>

			<div class="rightcol" id="ReviewContentsummary39386279_rightcol">
								<a href="https://steamcommunity.com/id/cyannuu/recommended/296070/" class="vote_header tooltip" data-tooltip-text="阅读完整评测">
					<div class="thumb">
						<img id="votingImage" src="https://store.akamai.steamstatic.com/public/shared/images/userreviews/icon_thumbsDown_v6.png" width="40" height="40">
													<img class="responsive_voting_image" src="https://community.akamai.steamstatic.com/public/images/apphubs/bigpicture/thumbs_down_selected.png" width="40" height="40">
											</div>

										<img class="review_source tooltip" data-tooltip-text="产品是从 Steam 直接购买的" src="https://store.akamai.steamstatic.com/public/shared/images/userreviews/icon_review_steam.png">
					
					<div class="title ellipsis">不推荐</div>
										<div class="hours ellipsis">
						总时数 2.5 小时											</div>
									</a>
				
				
													<div class="responsive_review_leftcol_ctn" id="ReviewContentsummary39386279_leftcol_ctn"></div>
				
				<div class="postedDate">
					发布于：2018 年 1 月 16 日																					<div class="responsive_purchase_source">
															Steam 直接购买													</div>
									</div>

								
				<div class="content">
					这个故事告诉我们评价褒贬不一的游戏不要轻易尝试。其实这游戏，我买的时候看着商店的褒贬不一，然后看了看宣传图觉得画面不错就入了，打折的时候也不贵，想着应该没有那么糟糕嘛。然后我玩了几关一脸懵逼，就去看了视频攻略，想边看边玩，但还是放弃了。挂个卡就算了吧。而且解成就的点也很谜，虽然说成就图标还挺好看……但是我放弃。<br>故事可能是一个爸爸在飓风灾害里失去了女儿然后很心痛就开始漫长的精神之旅这种吧。<br><br>· 对晕3D选手来说很不友好，我玩了不到半小时就开始头晕，虽然这是玩家个人原因，不过还是很影响体验的。建议晕3D选手可以直接跳过这游戏了。这个步行模拟也不是某获奖作品那样流程不长而且游戏本身精美，让人就算晕3D也可以咬牙玩下来。<br>· 解谜因素因为没有提示对很多人来说不知所云，我看了两三章的视频攻略，总结一下解谜玩法：神经球是一个道具，放在三棵树中间或者发光的草地上可以起到和人站在上面一样的效果；有些路不是你看到的那样，是隐藏的，需要自己慢慢试；必要的时候可以把道具扔到另一边然后死一次复活来到地图另一个地方（某块地方里复活的地方是固定的）；风暴可以把你弹到比较高的地方；等等。但是就算知道了玩法以后也感觉有些无趣了。并且没有shift加速跑功能，很急。<br>· 最生气的就是虽然有中文字幕但是字非常非常非常非常非常小，仿佛视力表最底下一行，不如看英文字幕。让我想到塞伯利亚3了，虽然说这些做比较小众游戏的歪果厂商加了中文已经很不容易了，可是根本没法看啊！！！我好心痛！！！<br>· 居然还有一些不明所以的惊悚元素，比如那个呲呲响到处滚的黑色球和红色蝙蝠群之类的东西，但是我只觉得脑壳疼，没觉得心里一颤之类的。<br>· 看到有评论称之为艺术品我觉得是不合适的。首先好看的风景其实就那么几种；然后它想表达的东西，父亲的精神自愈过程，也很隐晦，我甚至怀疑精神之旅只是解谜内容和好看风景的一个架子罢了。实际上就是一个不明也不觉厉的作品。<br><br>综上所述我建议看到这篇评测的盆宇不要购买，好奇的话油管有完整通关视频可以看一看，自己玩还是有点糟心的。					<div class="gradient"></div>
				</div>

				<div class="content">
					请注意游戏的名字叫《心智：视丘之径（MIND: Path to Thalamus）》。<br><br>其实这个作者本来作品的风格就是精神病般的解谜和场景表现，注定不能为大部分人所接受。<br><br>不过在我看来里面的谜题设置倒是少见的严谨和循序渐进，至少是有逻辑的。<br><br>其实作者在一个解谜的框架下去构建了一个尽可能优美的世界，虽不至于上升到艺术的高度，但我很享受解谜和看风景的过程。<br>					<div class="gradient"></div>

				<div class="content">
					玩下来最大的感觉是唯美，壁纸级别的唯美。<br>不过游戏性方面似乎没有很大的出色，简单来说就是步行模拟器。边走边欣赏风景是这个游戏的一大乐趣。<br>不好的地方在于，游戏的光影，没光的地方太暗，直接影响到视线。还有我卡关了，我觉得这个游戏的提示不够。<br>————————————————<br>通关卸载之后的追加评论：这个游戏还有一个缺点，或者说针对我的缺点。那就是玩的太久会晕，晕车的晕，最后一关来来往往放个球搞得我胃都想吐了，可能这就是大家说的3D眩晕吧。					<div class="gradient"></div>

	<div data-panel="{&quot;type&quot;:&quot;PanelGroup&quot;}" class="review_box short   partial">
		<div id="ReviewContentrecent_short58365821">
			
			<a href="https://steamcommunity.com/id/fhfuih/recommended/296070/" class="short_header tooltip" data-tooltip-text="阅读完整评测">
									<img class="review_source tooltip" data-tooltip-text="产品是从 Steam 直接购买的" src="https://store.akamai.steamstatic.com/public/shared/images/userreviews/icon_review_steam.png">
								<div class="thumb">
					<img src="https://store.akamai.steamstatic.com/public/shared/images/userreviews/icon_thumbsDown_v6.png" width="40" height="40">
				</div>
				<div class="persona_name"><span data-miniprofile="189170005">fhfuih</span></div>
									<div class="hours ellipsis"> 0.7 小时</div>
							</a>

			
			<div class="shortcol" id="ReviewContentrecent_short58365821_shortcol">
				
				
													<div class="responsive_review_leftcol_ctn" id="ReviewContentrecent_short58365821_leftcol_ctn"></div>
				
				<div class="postedDate">
					发布于：2019 年 11 月 28 日																					<div class="responsive_purchase_source">
															Steam 直接购买													</div>
									</div>

								
				<div class="content">
					刚刚启动感觉比较看上去不错，叙事引导的步行模拟我玩过的也不少。一进去那个简单的视角迷宫和镜子谜题都不错，哪知道之后就给我扔到了一个黑不溜秋的山洞里面给我走迷宫，我特么下载这个游戏是冲着宣传片上面那么多超现实且美妙的场景去的，不是在这里一个在一个根本看不见、自己都不知道自己怎么走的迷宫里面浪费十几二十分钟的啊！好不容易走到了一个瀑布旁边的平台上，看到有一个门，进入之后给我传送到原地又是什么鬼？玩到这里真的非常心烦，手上还要拿着一个小球（解谜钥匙）找不着放置的地方，而且因为山洞里面太黑了不知道自己面前是墙是路，撞到墙了一挤，小球就掉在在地上了（没有物品栏，小球只能一直拿在手上举着）。<br>另外关于叙事，在迷宫入口处画面会打印出游戏标题，也就是说之前的镜子谜题什么的算一个序章。然而到了这里我已经知道故事是什么了。从“真正开始游戏”开始，我已经没有了玩游戏的驱动力，除非真的耐着心子走完迷宫之后会有新的“在超现实世界中的自我救赎”云云，但这不重要啊，现实世界发生了什么故事我已经知道了，后面即便是纯散步刻画主人公的懊悔情绪，又有多少区别呢？<br>所以我找到了这个游戏的速通方法：前往这款游戏的网站，看看有没有media kit或者高清截屏壁纸，下载，完事。<br><br>====<br><br>1. The simple perspective maze and the mirror puzzles at the beginning is quite good. Makes me feel promising and intrigued.<br>2. Then our character enters an EXTREMELY DARK maze in a cave, which I think completely ruins the game. I buy the game for its beautiful and surreal scenes in the screenshots, and now you ask me to first waste 20 minutes on a maze that I don't know where I am heading?<br>2.1. Eventually I found a door at a platform near a waterfall, I entered it but it TELEPORTS ME TO EXACTLY THE LOCATION OF THE DOOR ITSELF (the distance of a jump above, actually, but no difference).<br>2.2. In addition, I have to carry a ball (some key) with me and don't know where to place it BECAUSE I SEE NOTHING BUT BLACK. The game has no "inventory" so I have to raise the ball in front of me all the way. And since I don't know whether it is a wall in front of me, once I hit the wall, the hitbox of the ball is squeezed and the ball falls onto the ground so I have to pick it up again. <br>3. As for the narration, at the entrance of the cave maze, the game title is printed on the screen, so I assume all the simple puzzles before it are a prequel. But I HAVE ALREADY LEARNED THE ENTIRE STORY IN THE PREQUEL (at least the story in the real world, if our character will enter another surreal world later). So I lost the driving force to push me through the entire game. Imagine you have spent 20 minutes in this dark cave, and you realized you finish the maze just to see the character fantasize his redemption in his imagination which may have little influence on the background story you have learned in the prequel. I guess the speedrun of this game is to head towards the website, see if there are any media kit or HD screenshot wallpapers, download it, and that's it.					<div class="gradient"></div>
				</div>
